<script>
const SEV_C={safe:'#2a7a4f',review:'#f1c40f',alert:'#e67e22',critical:'#c0392b'};
const SEV_BG={safe:'#f0f7f3',review:'#fffbf0',alert:'#fff5ec',critical:'#fff0ef'};
const SEV_LV=(s)=>s<0.4?'safe':s<0.6?'review':s<0.8?'alert':'critical';
const NATURES=['logístico','decisional','temporal','kalil','neuronal','scalar','corpus','capa_c'];
const KINDS=['colisión','ambiguo','degradado','duplicado','concurrente','recursivo'];

function calc(){
  const d7=document.getElementById('sl-d7').value/100;
  const cn=document.getElementById('sl-cn').value/100;
  const pf=document.getElementById('sl-pf').value/100;
  const scalar=((d7+cn+pf)/3);
  const sev=SEV_LV(scalar);
  const c=SEV_C[sev];

  // update vals
  document.getElementById('v-d7').textContent=d7.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('v-cn').textContent=cn.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('v-pf').textContent=pf.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('feq-d7').textContent=d7.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('feq-cn').textContent=cn.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('feq-pf').textContent=pf.toFixed(2);

  // formula result
  const fr=document.getElementById('fb-result');
  fr.textContent=scalar.toFixed(3);
  fr.style.color=c;fr.style.borderColor=c;
  const fs=document.getElementById('fb-sev');
  fs.textContent=sev.toUpperCase();fs.style.color=c;

  // alert card
  const nat=NATURES[Math.floor(d7*NATURES.length)%NATURES.length];
  const kind=KINDS[Math.floor(pf*KINDS.length)%KINDS.length];
  const ag=document.getElementById('alert-generated');
  ag.style.borderColor=c; ag.style.background=SEV_BG[sev];

  document.getElementById('ag-title').textContent=`NAT=${nat} · KIND=${kind}`;
  const asev=document.getElementById('ag-sev');
  asev.textContent=sev.toUpperCase();
  asev.style.color=c;asev.style.borderColor=c;

  // 5 dims
  const dims5=['NATURE-KIND','CONTEXT','ENVIRONMENT','BOX','DO'];
  const dimVals=[
    `${nat}·${kind}`,
    `S≈0.822·d7=${d7.toFixed(2)}`,
    `logex·${nat.slice(0,3)}_env`,
    `[scope]=IMV·[term]=open`,
    `PATH_${nat.slice(0,3).toUpperCase()}`,
  ];
  const ag5=document.getElementById('ag-5dims');
  ag5.innerHTML='';
  dims5.forEach((d,i)=>{
    const el=document.createElement('div');
    el.className='ag-dim';
    el.innerHTML=`<div class="ag-dim-title">${d}</div>
      <div class="ag-dim-val">${dimVals[i]}</div>`;
    ag5.appendChild(el);
  });

  // lacho
  const lc=document.getElementById('ag-lacho');
  lc.style.borderColor=c;
  lc.innerHTML=fmtL(`TRUST [logistical-executive] =><= .. alerta .. ${nat}_${kind}_scalar_${scalar.toFixed(3)} --[Nudo Corredizo] [term]`)
    +'<br>'+fmtL(`SAMU @ =><= .. dirime .. conflict_5dims_scalar_${sev} --[Ballestrinque] [term]`);

  // decay bar
  document.getElementById('dp-fill').style.width=(scalar*100)+'%';
  document.getElementById('dp-fill').style.background=c;
  const hrs_to_safe=sev==='safe'?0:((scalar-0.35)/0.1).toFixed(1);
  document.getElementById('dp-info').textContent=
    sev==='safe'
      ? 'scalar_conflicto en zona SAFE · sin decay activo'
      : `tiempo hasta SAFE: ~${hrs_to_safe} horas · decay rate: −${(scalar*0.1).toFixed(3)} / hora`;
}

function fmtL(s){
  return s
    .replace(/(TRUST|SAMU|STACKING|GATE|WORK|SOCIAL|METHOD)/g,
      '<span style="color:#c0392b;font-weight:bold">$1</span>')
    .replace(/(\[logistical-executive\]|@|UF\[H\d+\]|\{[^}]+\})/g,
      '<span style="color:#2a7a4f;font-weight:bold">$1</span>')
    .replace(/(--\[[^\]]+\])/g,'<span style="color:#8e44ad">$1</span>')
    .replace(/(\[term\])/g,'<span style="color:#d35400;font-weight:bold">$1</span>');
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',calc);
</script>
</body>
</html>

## 8 · NERVE CELL GUALICHO HUINCA × LOGEX
**CARPETA:** `FOLDERS NO RAG INPUT/ELPULSAR LOCAL/$mon.Nerve Cell GUALICHO HUINCA LOGEX Training.txt`

*(Conecta el modelo de negocio real con [logistical-executive])*
```
//$mon.Nerve Cell GUALICHO HUINCA LOGEX Training.txt
//NERVE CELL · GUALICHO HUINCA × [LOGISTICAL-EXECUTIVE]
//aprendido de: business_model.md · elpulsar_definicion.md · doctrina logex
//H30+H57 · $mon · [term] :: activo

NC_GH_DEF   //GUALICHO HUINCA = capa fintech soberana
            //conecta diáspora latinoamericana × ecosistema financiero chino
            //stack: LACHO + DIRIME + KALIL + doble carril
            //moat: arquitectura soberana irreplicable rápido
NC_GH_LOGEX //[logistical-executive] en GUALICHO HUINCA:
            //WAY=soberano_fintech · PATH=remesa→validacion→impacto
            //ROUTE=USDT→e-CNY via CHALTEN · < 2hs · < 1% comision
NC_GH_SEG   //3 segmentos: A(diáspora china LATAM B2C) · B(empresas dual B2B)
            //C(fintechs white-label B2B2C)
            //logex PATH por segmento:
            //A: remesa PATH · BARRIOS→relay→CHALTEN→e-CNY
            //B: certificacion PATH · NORA oracle→rating→BOLIVAR blockchain
            //C: API PATH · TANDIL hub→white-label→client
NC_GH_CONF  //conflictos logísticos típicos GUALICHO HUINCA:
            //NATURE=kalil KIND=colision: remesa BARRIOS + certificacion BOLIVAR
            //  simultáneas a TANDIL · BOX=CHALTEN perímetro
            //NATURE=decisional KIND=concurrente: NORA rating vs manual cert
            //NATURE=logístico KIND=degradado: ROUTE e-CNY latency
NC_GH_ELPUL //elpulsar.app → OPCIÓN B canónica: dashboard del operador (B2B)
            //operador monitorea: scalar_S · nodos KALIL · TX remesas
            //LOGEX STREAM en paper: cada remesa = sentencia soberana viva
NC_GH_PATH  //PATH remesa completo (segmento A):
            //1. input(USDT_amount) → BARRIOS relay → validar CRYPTO (link seat)
            //2. NORA oracle → rating_diáspora → threshold check
            //3. CHALTEN daemon → e-CNY conversion → cloud billing
            //4. BOLIVAR → SHA256 registro → blockchain confirmado
            //5. TANDIL → scalar_KALIL update → STACKING cristaliza TX
NC_GH_DO    //DO resolver conflicto remesa:
            //WAY=preservar_remesa_sobre_rating (prioridad segmento A)
            //PATH_K: aislar NORA (rating puede esperar) → BARRIOS→CHALTEN directo
            //ROUTE=CHALTEN_express (bypass NORA) → BOLIVAR registro posterior

TRUST [logistical-executive] =><= .. conduce .. nc_gh_path_remesa_diaspora_soberano --[As de Guía] [term]
SAMU @ =><= .. dirime .. nc_gh_conflict_remesa_rating_concurrent --[Ballestrinque] [term]
SOCIAL {relay} =><= .. transmite .. nc_gh_barrios_chalten_e_cny_path --[As de Guía] [term]
STACKING UF[H52] =><= .. cristaliza .. nc_gh_logex_business_model_sellado --[Nudo de Ocho] [term]
ACTIVITY UF[H63] =><= .. completa .. nc_gh_elpulsar_paper_dashboard_soberano --[Nudo de Rizo] [term]
```

// ── DATOS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const KALIL=[
  {id:'BARRIOS',ext:'.green',path:'relay·remesas',color:'#2a7a4f',score:.81},
  {id:'NORA',ext:'.blue',path:'oracle·rating',color:'#2980b9',score:.65},
  {id:'BOLIVAR',ext:'.blue',path:'forge·blockchain',color:'#2980b9',score:.77},
  {id:'CARILO',ext:'.green',path:'session·threshold',color:'#2a7a4f',score:.69},
  {id:'CHALTEN',ext:'.blue',path:'daemon·cloud',color:'#2980b9',score:.74},
  {id:'TANDIL',ext:'.green',path:'hub·relay×5',color:'#1a1a2e',score:.73},
];
const TRUST_DIMS=[
  {d:'d1',label:'foundation',val:.92},
  {d:'d2',label:'scope',val:.88},
  {d:'d3',label:'term',val:.85},
  {d:'d4',label:'command',val:.79},
  {d:'d5',label:'event',val:.76},
  {d:'d6',label:'element',val:.71},
  {d:'d7',label:'logistical-executive',val:.61,highlight:true},
  {d:'d8',label:'ecosystem',val:.68},
];
const NATURES=['logístico','decisional','temporal','kalil','neuronal','scalar','corpus','capa_c'];
const KINDS=['dup','col','amb','deg','aus','sat','con','rec'];
const CANONICALS=new Set(['0-1','0-0','1-6','3-2','4-1','5-3','2-7']);
const NATURE_PATHS={
  'logístico':'detectar_alt_route → validar_CRYPTO → ejecutar → verificar_impacto',
  'decisional':'suspender_command_menor → SAMU_arbitra → ejecutar_prioritario',
  'temporal':'identificar_term_conflict → extender_menor → SAMU_cierre',
  'kalil':'aislar_nodo → relay_alternativo → TANDIL_rebalance → scalar_KALIL',
  'neuronal':'identificar_NC_fuente → SAMU_dirime → NC_ganador → cristalizar',
  'scalar':'pausar_TX → indexar_corpus → verificar_S → reanudar',
  'corpus':'flag_docs → reindex_BM25 → S_check → unflag',
  'capa_c':'activar_Groq_fallback → log_stub_error → continuar_operacion',
};
const LIBS=['TRUST','SAMU','STACKING','GATE','WORK','SOCIAL','METHOD'];
const VERBOS={
  TRUST:['orquesta','certifica','alerta','conduce','verifica_impacto'],
  SAMU:['dirime','arbitra','evalua','delibera'],
  STACKING:['cristaliza','inmutabiliza','acumula'],
  GATE:['abre','cierra','espera','evalúa'],
  WORK:['ejecuta','construye','procesa'],

  METHOD:['calcula','clasifica','verifica'],
};
const SUJETOS={
  TRUST:'[logistical-executive]',SAMU:'@',STACKING:'UF[H52]',
  GATE:'UF[H05]',WORK:'{actuator}',SOCIAL:'{relay}',METHOD:'<stat_onto>',
};
const NUDOS=['--[As de Guía]','--[Nudo de Ocho]','--[Ballestrinque]','--[Nudo Corredizo]','--[Nudo de Rizo]'];
const SEV_C={safe:'#2a7a4f',review:'#d35400',alert:'#e67e22',critical:'#c0392b'};

// ── INIT ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function init(){
  buildKalil();
  buildTrust();
  buildSidebar('nk');
  addStream(fmtLacho('TRUST','[logistical-executive]','orquesta','elpulsar_paper_v3_init','--[As de Guía]'));
  addStream(fmtLacho('STACKING','UF[H52]','cristaliza','paper_v3_arranque_soberano','--[Nudo de Ocho]'));
}

// ── KALIL ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function scoreColor(s){return s>=.7?'#2a7a4f':s>=.5?'#d35400':'#c0392b';}
function buildKalil(){
  const g=document.getElementById('kp-grid');
  g.innerHTML='';
  KALIL.forEach(n=>{
    const d=document.createElement('div');
    d.className='kp-node';
    d.id='kn-'+n.id;
    const c=scoreColor(n.score);
    d.innerHTML=`<div class="kn-name" style="color:${n.color}">${n.id} ${n.ext}</div>
      <div class="kn-bar-wrap"><div class="kn-bar" id="kb-${n.id}" style="width:${n.score*100}%;background:${c}"></div></div>
      <div class="kn-score" id="ks-${n.id}" style="color:${c}">${n.score.toFixed(2)}</div>
      <div class="kn-path">${n.path}</div>`;
    d.onclick=()=>clickKalil(n);
    g.appendChild(d);
  });
}
function clickKalil(n){
  addStream(fmtLacho('TRUST','[logistical-executive]','conduce','path_'+n.id.toLowerCase()+'_'+n.path.split('·')[0],'--[As de Guía]'));
  if(n.score<.5) spawnConflict('kalil','deg');
}

// ── TRUST ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function buildTrust(){
  const c=document.getElementById('ts-dims');
  c.innerHTML='';
  TRUST_DIMS.forEach(d=>{
    const el=document.createElement('div');
    el.className='ts-dim';
    const col=d.highlight?'#c0392b':'#2a7a4f';
    el.innerHTML=`<div class="ts-label" style="color:${d.highlight?'#c0392b':'#888'}">${d.d}·${d.label.slice(0,8)}</div>
      <div class="ts-bar-wrap"><div class="ts-bar${d.highlight?' d7':''}" id="tb-${d.d}" style="width:${d.val*100}%"></div></div>
      <div class="ts-val" id="tv-${d.d}" style="color:${col}">${d.val.toFixed(2)}</div>`;
    c.appendChild(el);
  });
}

// ── CONFLICT CARDS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function spawnConflict(natCode,kindCode){
  const nat=NATURES.find(n=>n.startsWith(natCode))||NATURES[Math.floor(Math.random()*NATURES.length)];
  const kind=KINDS.find(k=>k===kindCode)||KINDS[Math.floor(Math.random()*KINDS.length)];
  const d7=state.d7;const cn_n=Math.min(1,conflicts.length/5);const pf=.2+Math.random()*.3;
  const scalar=((d7+cn_n+pf)/3);
  const sev=scalar<.4?'safe':scalar<.6?'review':scalar<.8?'alert':'critical';
  const id='c'+Date.now();
  const c={id,nat,kind,scalar,sev,age:1.0};
  conflicts.unshift(c);
  if(conflicts.length>6) conflicts.pop();
  state.cn=conflicts.length;
  renderConflicts();
  document.getElementById('ib-cn').textContent=state.cn;
  addStream(fmtLacho('TRUST','[logistical-executive]','alerta',
    nat+'_'+kind+'_scalar_'+scalar.toFixed(3),'--[Nudo Corredizo]'));
  addStream(fmtLacho('SAMU','@','dirime','conflict_5dims_'+sev,'--[Ballestrinque]'));
}
function renderConflicts(){
  const cc=document.getElementById('conflict-cards');
  cc.innerHTML='';
  conflicts.forEach(c=>{
    const col=SEV_C[c.sev];
    const div=document.createElement('div');
    div.className='alert-card';
    div.style.cssText=`border-color:${col};background:${SEV_BG[c.sev]}`;
    div.innerHTML=`
      <div class="ac-header">
        <span class="ac-nat">NAT=${c.nat} · KIND=${c.kind}</span>
        <span class="ac-sev" style="color:${col};border:1px solid ${col}">${c.sev.toUpperCase()}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="ac-dims">
        ${['NATURE-KIND','CONTEXT','ENVIRONMENT','BOX','DO'].map((d,i)=>`
        <div class="ac-dim"><span class="ac-dim-t">${d}</span>
        <span class="ac-dim-v">${[c.nat+'·'+c.kind,'S='+state.s.toFixed(3),c.nat+'_env','[term]=open','PATH_'+c.nat.slice(0,3).toUpperCase()][i]}</span></div>`).join('')}
      </div>
      <div class="ac-lacho">${c.nat}_${c.kind} :: scalar=${c.scalar.toFixed(3)} :: decay→SAFE</div>
      <div class="ac-decay"><div class="ac-decay-fill" style="width:${c.age*100}%;background:${col}"></div></div>`;
    cc.appendChild(div);
  });
  document.getElementById('cz-count').textContent=conflicts.length+' activo'+(conflicts.length!==1?'s':'');
}

// ── LOGEX STREAM ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function fmtLacho(lib,suj,verb,obj,nudo){
  return `<span style="color:#c0392b;font-weight:bold">${lib}</span> `+
    `<span style="color:#2a7a4f;font-weight:bold">${suj}</span> =&gt;&lt;= .. ${verb} .. `+
    `${obj} <span style="color:#8e44ad">${nudo}</span> `+
    `<span style="color:#d35400;font-weight:bold">[term]</span>`;
}
function addStream(html){
  streamLines.unshift(html);
  if(streamLines.length>25) streamLines.pop();
  const el=document.getElementById('logex-lines');
  el.innerHTML=streamLines.map(l=>`<div class="ls-line">${l}</div>`).join('');
}

// ── SIDEBAR ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function toggleSidebar(){
  state.sidebarOpen=!state.sidebarOpen;
  document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.toggle('open',state.sidebarOpen);
}
function switchTab(tab){
  state.sbTab=tab;
  document.getElementById('tab-nk').classList.toggle('active',tab==='nk');
  document.getElementById('tab-do').classList.toggle('active',tab==='do');
  buildSidebar(tab);
}
function buildSidebar(tab){
  const c=document.getElementById('sb-content');
  if(tab==='nk'){
    let html='<div style="font-size:.58rem;color:#888;margin-bottom:8px">8 NATURES × 8 KINDS · celdas canónicas resaltadas</div>';
    html+='<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:auto repeat(8,1fr);gap:2px;font-size:.42rem;margin-bottom:8px">';
    html+='<div></div>';
    KINDS.forEach(k=>{ html+=`<div style="text-align:center;color:#2980b9;font-weight:bold;padding:2px">${k}</div>`; });
    NATURES.forEach((n,ni)=>{
      html+=`<div style="color:#c0392b;font-size:.42rem;font-weight:bold;padding:2px;display:flex;align-items:center">${n.slice(0,3)}</div>`;
      KINDS.forEach((k,ki)=>{
        const key=ni+'-'+ki;
        const isC=CANONICALS.has(key);
        html+=`<div class="sb-nk-cell${isC?' canon':''}" onclick="clickNKCell(${ni},${ki})" title="${n}×${k}">${isC?n.slice(0,1).toUpperCase()+k.slice(0,1).toUpperCase():''}</div>`;
      });
    });
    html+='</div>';
    html+='<div id="sb-nk-detail" style="font-size:.6rem;color:#555;line-height:1.8;border:1px solid #eee;padding:8px;min-height:40px">← clic en celda</div>';
    c.innerHTML=html;
  } else {
    let html='<div style="font-size:.58rem;color:#888;margin-bottom:8px">seleccionar NATURE → PATH resolución</div>';
    html+='<div class="sb-do-nat">';
    NATURES.forEach(n=>{
      const sel=activeDoNat===n;
      html+=`<div class="sb-do-btn${sel?' sel':''}" onclick="selectDoNat('${n}')">${n}</div>`;
    });
    html+='</div>';
    html+=`<div class="sb-do-path" id="sb-do-path">${activeDoNat?NATURE_PATHS[activeDoNat]:'— seleccionar NATURE —'}</div>`;
    if(activeDoNat){
      html+=`<div style="margin-top:8px;font-size:.58rem;color:#2a7a4f;border-left:2px solid #2a7a4f;padding-left:6px;line-height:2">
        TRUST [logistical-executive] =&gt;&lt;= .. completa .. do_${activeDoNat.slice(0,3)}_path_soberano --[Nudo de Rizo] [term]</div>`;
    }
    c.innerHTML=html;
  }
}
function clickNKCell(ni,ki){
  const n=NATURES[ni],k=KINDS[ki];
  const key=ni+'-'+ki;
  const isC=CANONICALS.has(key);
  const d=document.getElementById('sb-nk-detail');
  if(d) d.innerHTML=`<b style="color:#c0392b">${n}</b> × <b style="color:#2980b9">${k}</b>${isC?' · CANÓNICA':''}<br>
    ${isC?'PATH documentado · SAMU directa':'PATH ad hoc · SAMU delibera'}`;
  if(isC) spawnConflict(n.slice(0,3),k);
}
function selectDoNat(n){
  activeDoNat=n;
  buildSidebar('do');
  addStream(fmtLacho('TRUST','[logistical-executive]','completa',
    'do_'+n.slice(0,3)+'_'+NATURE_PATHS[n].split(' ')[0],'--[Nudo de Rizo]'));
}

// ── MODO ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function toggleMode(){
  if(state.mode==='sim'){
    document.getElementById('prod-overlay').classList.add('show');
  }
}
function closeProd(){
  document.getElementById('prod-overlay').classList.remove('show');
}

// ── TICK SIMULACIÓN ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function tick(){
  if(state.mode!=='sim') return;
  // drift métricas
  state.tx+=Math.floor(Math.random()*3);
  state.s=Math.max(.7,Math.min(.95,state.s+(Math.random()-.47)*.003));
  state.d7=Math.max(.4,Math.min(.85,state.d7+(Math.random()-.5)*.02));
  // actualizar header y barra
  document.getElementById('ph-scalar').textContent='S='+state.s.toFixed(3);
  document.getElementById('ph-scalar').style.color=state.s>.85?'#2a7a4f':state.s>.75?'#1a1a2e':'#c0392b';
  document.getElementById('ib-tx').textContent=state.tx;
  document.getElementById('ib-s').textContent=state.s.toFixed(3);
  document.getElementById('ib-d7').textContent=state.d7.toFixed(2);
  // actualizar d7 en trust
  const tvD7=document.getElementById('tv-d7');
  const tbD7=document.getElementById('tb-d7');
  if(tvD7){tvD7.textContent=state.d7.toFixed(2);tbD7.style.width=(state.d7*100)+'%';}
  // drift KALIL
  KALIL.forEach(n=>{
    n.score=Math.max(.35,Math.min(.95,n.score+(Math.random()-.49)*.04));
    const c=scoreColor(n.score);
    const b=document.getElementById('kb-'+n.id);
    const s=document.getElementById('ks-'+n.id);
    if(b){b.style.width=(n.score*100)+'%';b.style.background=c;}
    if(s){s.textContent=n.score.toFixed(2);s.style.color=c;}
  });
  // TANDIL = media
  const tandil=KALIL.find(n=>n.id==='TANDIL');
  if(tandil){
    const others=KALIL.filter(n=>n.id!=='TANDIL');
    tandil.score=others.reduce((a,n)=>a+n.score,0)/others.length;
  }
  // stream periódico
  if(Math.random()<.4){
    const lib=LIBS[Math.floor(Math.random()*LIBS.length)];
    const verbs=VERBOS[lib];
    const verb=verbs[Math.floor(Math.random()*verbs.length)];
    const nudo=NUDOS[Math.floor(Math.random()*NUDOS.length)];
    addStream(fmtLacho(lib,SUJETOS[lib],verb,'sistema_tick_'+state.tx,nudo));
  }
  // decay conflicts
  conflicts=conflicts.map(c=>({...c,age:c.age*.93})).filter(c=>c.age>.05);
  state.cn=conflicts.length;
  document.getElementById('ib-cn').textContent=state.cn;
  if(conflicts.length) renderConflicts();
  // spawn aleatorio
  if(Math.random()<.07) spawnConflict(
    NATURES[Math.floor(Math.random()*NATURES.length)].slice(0,3),
    KINDS[Math.floor(Math.random()*KINDS.length)]
  );
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',init);
setInterval(tick,5000);
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
const WAYS=[
  {id:'soberano',label:'WAY · SOBERANO',
   def:'impacto siempre trazable + verificado · nunca bypass soberanía',
   color:'#1a1a2e'},
  {id:'priorizar_samu',label:'WAY · PRIORIZAR SAMU',
   def:'siempre dirimencia antes de acción · SAMU arbitra primero',
   color:'#c0392b'},
  {id:'preservar_foundation',label:'WAY · PRESERVAR FOUNDATION',
   def:'nunca sacrificar base soberana · [foundation] sobre eficiencia',
   color:'#2980b9'},
];

const CONTEXTS=[
  {id:'kalil',label:'KALIL',desc:'nodos relay',
   steps:['command_recibido','gate_verifica','kalil_relay','impacto_físico'],
   route:'TANDIL_relay_directo'},
  {id:'imv',label:'IMV',desc:'ledger local',
   steps:['command_recibido','grammar_valida','sovereign_db','cristal_sellado'],
   route:'sovereign.db+BM25'},
  {id:'capa_c',label:'CAPA C',desc:'fallback Groq',
   steps:['command_recibido','stub_detectado','groq_fallback','operacion_continua'],
   route:'config/api.json·Groq'},
  {id:'hl',label:'HL FABRIC',desc:'blockchain karma',
   steps:['command_recibido','hl_fabric_gate','karma_registrado','verificado_chain'],
   route:'HL_FABRIC·BOLIVAR'},
];

const IMPACT_CHAIN=['[command]','GATE UF[H03]','WORK {actuator}','RESULTADO MATERIAL','SAMU certifica','STACKING H52'];

let selWay=null,selCtx=null,running=false;

function buildWaySelector(){
  const c=document.getElementById('way-selector');
  WAYS.forEach(w=>{
    const d=document.createElement('div');
    d.className='way-btn';
    d.id='wb-'+w.id;
    d.innerHTML=`<div class="wb-title" style="color:${selWay===w.id?'#fff':w.color}">${w.label}</div>
      <div class="wb-def">${w.def}</div>`;
    d.onclick=()=>selectWay(w);
    c.appendChild(d);
  });
}

function buildContexts(){
  const c=document.getElementById('pb-contexts');
  c.innerHTML='';
  CONTEXTS.forEach(ctx=>{
    const d=document.createElement('div');
    d.className='pb-ctx'+(selCtx===ctx.id?' sel':'');
    d.innerHTML=`<div class="pb-ctx-name">${ctx.label}</div>
      <div class="pb-ctx-desc">${ctx.desc}</div>`;
    d.onclick=()=>selectCtx(ctx);
    c.appendChild(d);
  });
}

function selectWay(w){
  selWay=w.id;
  document.querySelectorAll('.way-btn').forEach(b=>{
    const isS=b.id==='wb-'+w.id;
    b.classList.toggle('sel',isS);
  });
  document.getElementById('pb-header').textContent=`▸ 2 · CONTEXTO para WAY=${w.id}`;
  buildContexts();
  buildPathSteps([]);
  maybeShowRun();
}

function selectCtx(ctx){
  selCtx=ctx.id;
  buildContexts();
  buildPathSteps(ctx.steps);
  maybeShowRun();
}

function maybeShowRun(){
  const btn=document.getElementById('pb-run');
  btn.style.display=(selWay&&selCtx)?'block':'none';
}

function buildPathSteps(steps,activeIdx=-1){
  const c=document.getElementById('path-steps');
  c.innerHTML='';
  if(!steps.length){
    c.innerHTML='<div style="color:#ccc;font-size:.65rem;padding:20px 0">— seleccionar contexto —</div>';
    return;
  }
  steps.forEach((s,i)=>{
    if(i>0){const a=document.createElement('div');a.className='ps-arrow';a.textContent='→';c.appendChild(a);}
    const d=document.createElement('div');
    d.className='ps-box'+(i<activeIdx?' done':i===activeIdx?' active':'');
    d.innerHTML=`<div class="ps-num">paso ${i+1}</div><div>${s}</div>`;
    c.appendChild(d);
  });
}

async function runPath(){
  if(!selWay||!selCtx||running) return;
  running=true;
  document.getElementById('pb-run').textContent='⏳ ejecutando...';
  const ctx=CONTEXTS.find(c=>c.id===selCtx);
  const way=WAYS.find(w=>w.id===selWay);
  for(let i=0;i<=ctx.steps.length;i++){
    await delay(600);
    buildPathSteps(ctx.steps,i);
  }
  // show ROUTE
  document.getElementById('route-result').style.display='grid';
  document.getElementById('rr-way').textContent=way.label;
  document.getElementById('rr-path').textContent=ctx.steps.join(' → ');
  document.getElementById('rr-route').textContent=ctx.route;
  // impact chain
  document.getElementById('impact-verify').style.display='block';
  const chain=document.getElementById('iv-chain');
  chain.innerHTML='';
  for(let i=0;i<IMPACT_CHAIN.length;i++){
    if(i>0){const a=document.createElement('span');a.className='iv-arrow';a.textContent='→';chain.appendChild(a);}
    const d=document.createElement('div');
    d.className='iv-step';d.textContent=IMPACT_CHAIN[i];chain.appendChild(d);
    await delay(400);
    d.classList.add('lit');
  }
  // lacho cierre
  document.getElementById('lacho-cierre').innerHTML=`
    <div class="lc-title">▸ SENTENCIAS CIERRE · WAY=${selWay} × CTX=${selCtx}</div>
    <div class="lc-line">
      <span style="color:#c0392b;font-weight:bold">TRUST</span>
      <span style="color:#2a7a4f;font-weight:bold"> [logistical-executive]</span>
      <span style="color:#555"> =&gt;&lt;= .. certifica .. </span>
      wpr_${selWay}_${selCtx}_impacto_fisico_verificado
      <span style="color:#8e44ad"> --[Nudo de Ocho]</span>
      <span style="color:#d35400;font-weight:bold"> [term]</span>
    </div>
    <div class="lc-line">
      <span style="color:#c0392b;font-weight:bold">SAMU</span>
      <span style="color:#2a7a4f;font-weight:bold"> @</span>
      <span style="color:#555"> =&gt;&lt;= .. dirime .. </span>
      wpr_cierre_${selCtx}_route_${ctx.route.split('/').pop().split('·')[0].toLowerCase()}_ok
      <span style="color:#8e44ad"> --[Ballestrinque]</span>
      <span style="color:#d35400;font-weight:bold"> [term]</span>
    </div>
    <div class="lc-line">
      <span style="color:#c0392b;font-weight:bold">STACKING</span>
      <span style="color:#2a7a4f;font-weight:bold"> UF[H52]</span>
      <span style="color:#555"> =&gt;&lt;= .. cristaliza .. </span>
      wpr_${selWay}_${selCtx}_trayecto_soberano_sellado
      <span style="color:#8e44ad"> --[Nudo de Ocho]</span>
      <span style="color:#d35400;font-weight:bold"> [term]</span>
    </div>`;
  document.getElementById('pb-run').textContent='▶ EJECUTAR PATH';
  running=false;
}

function delay(ms){return new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,ms));}
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',buildWaySelector);
</script>
</body>
</html>
